<script>
    
    function selectVideo(vid) {
        var videoIndex = window.videoPlaylist.findIndex(playlistItem => playlistItem.mediaid === vid);
        var selectedPlaylistItem = window.videoPlaylist.splice(videoIndex, 1)[0];
        window.videoPlaylist.unshift(selectedPlaylistItem);
    }

(function(){

if(window.jwplayer) {
    var site = window.page.toLowerCase() === 'everydaylife' ? 'EVERYDAYLIFE' : 'FRONTPAGE'
    var p = window.jwplayer();
    p.on('ready', function(){

        p.on('playlistItem', function(event){
            window.subsequentVideoId = event.item.mediaid;
            });

        p.on('adImpression', function () {
            PCHGA.trackEvent(site + "/VideoAd", 'VideoAdImp', window.location.href + '/' + window.subsequentVideoId);
        });

        p.on('adError', function () {
            PCHGA.trackEvent(site + "/VideoAd", 'Error', window.location.href + '/' + window.subsequentVideoId);
        });

        p.on('play', function () {
            PCHGA.trackEvent(site + "/Video", 'Start', window.location.href + '/' + window.subsequentVideoId);
        });

        p.on('complete', function () {
            PCHGA.trackEvent(site + "/Video", 'Complete', window.location.href + '/' + window.subsequentVideoId);
        });

        p.on('error setupError', function () {
            PCHGA.trackEvent(site + "/Video", 'Error', window.location.href + '/' + window.subsequentVideoId);
        });

        if(window.HEALTHINATION && window.HEALTHINATION.comscoreConfig && ns_ && ns_.StreamingAnalytics) {
            ns_.StreamingAnalytics.JWPlayer(p, HEALTHINATION.comscoreConfig);
        }
    });
}

})();
